## Routing & Navigation Map (derived from actual code)
- Routing system: React Router v6 (BrowserRouter)
- Route tree:
	- / → LandingPage
	- /reset-password → ResetPassword
	- /update-password → UpdatePassword
	- /onboarding → UserOnboarding
	- /onboarding/profile → ProfileOnboarding (ProtectedRoute with relaxed requirements)
	- /dashboard → Dashboard (ProtectedRoute)
	- /projects/:id → ProjectDashboard (ProtectedRoute)
	- /projects/:id/settings → ContractSettings (ProtectedRoute)
	- /projects/create → ContractCreation (ProtectedRoute)
	- /calculators → Calculators (ProtectedRoute)
	- /calculators/usage → CalculatorUsage (ProtectedRoute)
	- /calculators/create → CalculatorCreation (ProtectedRoute)
	- /changeorders → ChangeOrders (ProtectedRoute)
	- /equipmentlog → EquipmentLog (ProtectedRoute)
	- /inspections → Inspections (ProtectedRoute)
	- /issues → Issues (ProtectedRoute)
	- /dailyreports → DailyReports (ProtectedRoute)
	- /projects → Projects (ProtectedRoute)
	- /estimates → Estimates (ProtectedRoute)
	- /cost-codes → CostCodes (ProtectedRoute)
	- /schedule-tasks → ScheduleTasks (ProtectedRoute)
	- /preconstruction → PreconstructionBidding (ProtectedRoute)
	- /document-management → DocumentManagement (ProtectedRoute)
	- /financial-management → FinancialManagement (ProtectedRoute)
	- /field-operations → FieldOperations (ProtectedRoute)
	- /equipment-management → EquipmentManagement (ProtectedRoute)
	- /design-reviews → DesignReviews (ProtectedRoute)
	- /equipment-maintenance → EquipmentMaintenance (ProtectedRoute)
	- /accounting-payroll → AccountingPayroll (ProtectedRoute)
	- /accounts-payable → AccountsPayable (ProtectedRoute)
	- /accounts-receivable → AccountsReceivable (ProtectedRoute)
	- /payments → Payments (ProtectedRoute)
	- /resource-planning → ResourcePlanning (ProtectedRoute)
	- /reporting → ReportingCollaboration (ProtectedRoute)
	- /quality-safety → QualitySafety (ProtectedRoute)
	- /subcontractors → SubcontractorManagement (ProtectedRoute)
	- /organizations → OrganizationDashboard (ProtectedRoute)
	- /organizations/onboarding → OrganizationOnboarding (ProtectedRoute requireOrganization=false)
	- * → NotFoundPage
- Layout shells: Navbar rendered in App for all routes except auth-style routes; ScrollToTop always mounted.

## Duplicates & Merge Plan
- UI button duplication:
	- src/components/ui/button.tsx vs src/pages/StandardPages/StandardPageComponents/button.tsx
	- Canonical: choose a single shared button component
	- Plan: compare APIs/styles; migrate imports to canonical; delete duplicate.
- Modal/dialog duplication:
	- src/components/ui/dialog.tsx vs src/pages/StandardPages/StandardPageComponents/modal.tsx
	- Canonical: choose shared modal/dialog implementation
	- Plan: align APIs; migrate usages; remove duplicate.
- Export helpers duplication:
	- src/components/ui/export-data.ts vs src/lib/utils/export-utils.ts
	- Canonical: src/lib/utils/export-utils.ts
	- Plan: merge helper functions; update imports; remove duplicate file.
- Issues page duplication:
	- src/pages/Projects/Issues.tsx vs src/pages/Projects/Issues_Fixed.tsx
	- Canonical: src/pages/Projects/Issues.tsx
	- Plan: diff for fixes; port improvements; remove Issues_Fixed.tsx if unused.
- Potential hook overlap:
	- useLocationSuggestions vs usePlacesAutocomplete
	- Plan: compare API calls; consolidate if identical.

## Dead/Unused Code Candidates (with evidence)
- src/pages/Projects/Issues_Fixed.tsx — not referenced by App routes; likely duplicate (confidence: MED)
- src/pages/Projects/LaborRecords.tsx — not referenced by App routes (confidence: MED)
- scripts/clean-next.cjs — not referenced in package.json scripts (confidence: HIGH)
- deno.lock — no Deno scripts in package.json (confidence: HIGH)
- src/components/FeatureListPage.tsx — no route references; import usage not found (confidence: LOW)

## Auth & Access Control Review
- Auth bootstraps via useBootstrapAuth in App and useAuthStore for state.
- Guards implemented in ProtectedRoute component; most routes are protected.
- Risk: hooks that call RPCs may fire before session is fully initialized (StrictMode double-invoke). Use guard checks or gate data fetching on auth readiness.
- Recommendation: standardize a single “auth-ready” hook and use it in data hooks before any RPC calls.

## Supabase Data Layer Review
- RPCs observed in code:
	- filter_projects (useDashboardMetrics, useProjectsData, Inspections)
	- insert_line_items, filter_line_items (EditableLineItemsTable)
	- filter_wbs, filter_maps (Inspections)
	- getContractWithWkt, getProfilesByContract, removeProfileFromContract, updateProfileContractRole (ContractSettings warnings)
- Missing RPC handling: warnMissingRpc used; consider hard failures for required RPCs.
- RLS/policy dependencies: not inspected here; ensure RPCs require auth and role checks.
- Risk: multiple RPC calls in single screen without caching; add memoization or batching.

## Performance & Reliability Review
- StrictMode double-invoke can trigger duplicate RPC calls (useBootstrapAuth, data hooks).
- Over-fetching risk: filter_* RPC calls in multiple hooks; consider caching and pagination.
- Global components (Analytics) appears twice in App; remove duplicate to avoid double reporting.
- Map components load heavy scripts; use lazy loading and memoized loaders.

## Consistency & Standards
- Naming consistency: duplicated UI components in separate folders; consolidate.
- Folder structure: UI components split between src/components/ui and StandardPageComponents; pick one.
- TypeScript: ensure no any usage; align with src/lib/database.types.ts.
- Suggested conventions: feature-specific components under src/features/<feature>/ and shared UI under src/components/ui.

## Fix Order (Priority)
- P0: remove duplicate Analytics render in src/App.tsx (avoids double analytics events).
- P1: resolve duplicate UI components (button/modal) and Issues page duplication.
- P1: standardize auth-ready gating for RPC hooks to prevent unauthorized calls.
- P2: clean up unused scripts/files (scripts/clean-next.cjs, deno.lock) after confirmation.
